                                              Attachment 18

                      CASUALTY NOTIFICATION OFFICER CHECKLIST

A18.1. Purpose of Notification. To provide dignified, compassionate and humane notification to family
members and other designated persons as promptly as possible after a member is placed in a casualty sta-
tus of deceased, Duty Status-Whereabouts Unknown (DUSTWUN), or Missing.

A18.2. Background.
   A18.2.1. This checklist provides guidance for preparing and completing casualty notifications.
   A18.2.2. A casualty notification will probably be one of the hardest duties you will perform in your
   military career.
   A18.2.3. You must convey, in every action and deed, the sincere concern of the Air Force for the feel-
   ings of the NOK.
   A18.2.4. Your duty as a casualty notification officer is to “soften the blow,” if possible, and to show
   that the Air Force is genuinely concerned about its members and their families.
   A18.2.5. Each notification is unique as a result of the individuals and circumstances surrounding the
   incident. We cannot cover all situations that you might encounter. We hope this checklist will provide
   enough information to assist you in preparing and completing a casualty notification and ease some of
   the anxiety often experienced by individuals when called upon to perform this sensitive task.
   A18.2.6. Remember, nothing can substitute for common sense, good judgment, and sensitivity in
   making a casualty notification.

A18.3. Casualty Notification Responsibility.
   A18.3.1. Air Force Personnel Center, Casualty Services Branch (AFPC/DPFCS) assigns the Air
   Force activity (active Air Force, Air National Guard, United States Air Force Reserve, and Air Force
   Reserve Officer Training Corps) nearest to the next of kin’s (NOK) residence to accomplish the casu-
   alty notification.
   A18.3.2. If the NOK live on or near the member’s home installation, the member’s wing, group,
   squadron commander, or other officer, as determined by the installation commander, effects personal
   notification to the NOK, provides circumstances surrounding the incident and expresses condolences.
   A18.3.3. The casualty notification duty:
       A18.3.3.1. Is on behalf of the Air Force Chief of Staff.
       A18.3.3.2. Has priority over all duties, except in emergencies.
       A18.3.3.3. Is accomplished in service dress uniform with the exception of the medical technician
       who can wear whites (he/she remains in the vehicle).

A18.4. Notification Team Composition.
   A18.4.1. Field grade officers, of equal or higher grade than the member about whom they are making
   notification, are assigned the responsibility for personal notification as directed by the installation
234                                                      AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


      commander or AFPC, Chief, Casualty Services Branch (AFPC/DPFCS). EXCEPTION: AFPC/
      DPFCS may assign other officers to notification duty.
         A18.4.1.1. Medical personnel (i.e., doctor, nurse, or medical technician) and an Air Force chap-
         lain, if available, accompany the notification officer to attend to any reaction of the NOK.
             A18.4.1.1.1. Notification should not be delayed due to the inability to obtain a medical officer
             or chaplain.
      A18.4.2. The commander or notification officer may invite another person to accompany the notifica-
      tion team such as a friend, co-worker or clergy/leader from the member’s faith community, known by
      the member’s family whose presence may be comforting to the family, if it does not delay the notifi-
      cation process.
      A18.4.3. On active duty installations, notification team members normally assemble in the casualty
      assistance representative’s (CAR) office within 30-45 minutes after receiving the telephone call from
      the CAR.
         A18.4.3.1. In most instances, an error-free notification letter has already been prepared and is
         ready for the notification officer to deliver to the NOK.
         A18.4.3.2. A notification letter is not required when the member’s commander or a designated
         representative personally notifies the NOK.

A18.5. Transportation.
      A18.5.1. The CAR, with help from the vehicle dispatcher, provides a military vehicle, sedan,
      mini-van or other appropriate vehicle for the notification officer.
         A18.5.1.1. Geographically separated unit (GSU) commanders establish arrangements for use of a
         government vehicle if available.
      A18.5.2. Notification officers must use military vehicles when available; otherwise, use of a privately
      owned vehicle (POV) is authorized.
         A18.5.2.1. When travel must be performed using a POV, the notification officer submits SF
         1164, Claim for Reimbursement for Expenditures on Official Business, to their servicing
         financial services office for reimbursement of expenses.
         A18.5.2.2. Reimbursement of expenses is chargeable to unit operation and maintenance (O&M)
         funds.

A18.6. Communication Support.
      A18.6.1. The military personnel flight (MPF) or GSU commander, with the help of support agencies,
      provides a cellular telephone or two-way radio for use by the notification officer or team.
      A18.6.2. The immediate availability to communicate with your installation casualty office and
      AFPC/DPFCS is necessary should you or the team encounter obstacles that prevent effecting and con-
      firming notifications in a timely manner.

A18.7. Preparing to Perform Casualty Notifications.
      A18.7.1. Review the DoD film, Casualty Notification.
AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007                                                                  235


   A18.7.2. Review AFI 36-3002, Chapter 3, Casualty Notifications.
   A18.7.3. Ensure your service dress uniform is in good condition. You must wear it for all casualty
   notifications.
   A18.7.4. Talk to your servicing MPF CAR to familiarize yourself with the Air Force Casualty Pro-
   gram and any unique local casualty notification procedures.
   A18.7.5. Talk to other field grade officers who have performed a casualty notification. Their experi-
   ences might help you prepare to perform this sensitive task.
   A18.7.6. Understand that your commander could call on you to perform a casualty notification at any
   time: Be prepared.

A18.8. Guidelines During the Pre-notification Phase.
   A18.8.1. Once your installation commander or HQ AFPC//DPFCS selects you for casualty notifica-
   tion duty, learn as much as you can about the casualty, the NOK, and the circumstances surrounding
   the incident.
   A18.8.2. The installation CAR or HQ AFPC/DPFCS will provide you with:
      A18.8.2.1. The notification procedures briefing.
      A18.8.2.2. The notification letter.
          A18.8.2.2.1. If assigned to a military installation, the CAR will give you the appropriate noti-
          fication letter.
          A18.8.2.2.2. If assigned to a GSU, HQ AFPC/DPFCS will fax or e-mail the appropriate noti-
          fication letter for your signature.
              A18.8.2.2.2.1. If faxed, you must retype verbatim and error-free (see AFI 36-3002, Chap-
              ter 3, paragraph 3.16., and Attachment 19 and Attachment 20, for further information).
          A18.8.2.2.3. This letter provides condolences on behalf of the Air Force and known circum-
          stances surrounding the incident.
          A18.8.2.2.4. You will take the original copy of the notification letter when you go to see the
          NOK.
      A18.8.2.3. The NOK’s name, relationship, and address, and any special conditions you will need
      to know (e.g., age, ill health, or precarious location of NOK).
      A18.8.2.4. Instructions if problems occur.
      A18.8.2.5. Map of the area, if available.
      A18.8.2.6. Transportation.
      A18.8.2.7. Cellular telephone or two-way radio.
      A18.8.2.8. HQ AFPC/DPFCS toll-free number (1-800-433-0048).
   A18.8.3. Familiarize yourself with the location of the NOK, the circumstances of the incident, and
   the notification letter.
236                                                     AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


         A18.8.3.1. If you are unsure of the NOK's location, ask the CAR, HQ AFPC/DPFCS, or local
         authorities for help.
         A18.8.3.2. If the NOK reside within an area where your safety may be threatened, request a
         police escort.

A18.9. Inability to Locate the NOK.
      A18.9.1. If it appears the NOK is not at home, you should contact neighbors, law enforcement agen-
      cies, or the local postmaster (not a postal clerk) for information regarding the NOK’s whereabouts.
      A18.9.2. If you or the team cannot locate the NOK, or the NOK has moved from the area, you should
      immediately telephone HQ AFPC/DPFCS toll-free at 1-800-433-0048 for further guidance and pro-
      vide the information concerning attempts to contact the NOK.

A18.10. Making the Notification.
      A18.10.1. A representative of the Air Force notifies the NOK in person whenever possible.
      A18.10.2. The Air Force honors the NOK’s wishes to notify other family members. EXAMPLE: If
      the spouse wishes to notify adult children or the parents.
      A18.10.3. If the NOK calls to ask about a member’s status before they receive official notification,
      AFPC/DPFCS, the member’s commander or a designated representative, or the CAR, tells the caller
      the member’s status during the call.
      A18.10.4. You must be alert to the needs of the NOK and represent the Air Force in a professional
      manner.
         A18.10.4.1. Being prepared, sincere, and alert to the needs of the family at time of notification
         will reduce some of the shock that is normal under these circumstances.
      A18.10.5. Stereotyped procedures are not appropriate.
      A18.10.6. As a minimum, you should:
         A18.10.6.1. Identify yourself to the NOK and any other members of the team. EXAMPLE: "I am
         Major Thompson and this is Major Jones from the 12th Mission Support Squadron at Randolph
         Air Force Base, Texas."
         A18.10.6.2. After identifying yourself, make sure you are speaking to the correct person(s) by
         confirming the identity of the NOK. EXAMPLE: "Are you Mr. Thomas Brown, the father of Staff
         Sergeant Carl Brown?"
         A18.10.6.3. If at least one person to be notified is home, you should state that you have an impor-
         tant message to deliver and ask permission to enter the residence.
         A18.10.6.4. Verbally relate to the NOK, without reading from the notification letter, the informa-
         tion contained in the letter, if applicable. EXAMPLE: “On behalf of the Chief of Staff, United
         States Air Force, I regret to inform you that your son, Staff Sergeant Carl Brown, died in Texas
         today as a result of injuries received in a motorcycle accident.” Then paraphrase any additional
         circumstances described in the notification letter.
         A18.10.6.5. Do not hurry the words; speak as naturally as possible.
AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007                                                                   237


       A18.10.6.6. Do not extend overly sympathetic gestures that may be taken the wrong way.
       A18.10.6.7. Do not physically touch the NOK in any manner other than to assist in an emergency.
       If necessary, summon the medical representative on the team or local emergency personnel.
       A18.10.6.8. Avoid making detailed statements about the incident.
       A18.10.6.9. Inform the NOK that the deceased member’s commander will send a letter explain-
       ing and confirming the circumstances surrounding the incident.
          A18.10.6.9.1. If you are the member’s commander or a designated representative and have
          first-hand knowledge of the circumstances, you may give the NOK additional information.
       A18.10.6.10. Inform the NOK eligible for casualty assistance that a casualty assistance represen-
       tative will contact them within 24 hours to arrange for a casualty assistance visit at their conve-
       nience.
       A18.10.6.11. Inform the NOK that:
          A18.10.6.11.1. For CONUS casualties, a mortuary affairs representative will contact them
          regarding mortuary affairs.
          A18.10.6.11.2. For overseas casualties, HQ Air Force Mortuary Services, San Antonio,
          Texas, will contact them regarding mortuary affairs.
       A18.10.6.12. Give the notification letter to the NOK, if applicable.
       A18.10.6.13. If the NOK have questions or need additional information, have them call HQ
       AFPC/DPFCS toll-free at 1-800-433-0048, and HQ AFPC/DPFCS will put the NOK in touch with
       their (husband’s, wife’s, son’s, daughter’s, father’s, or mother’s) commander.

A18.11. Information You Must Not Discuss With NOK.
   A18.11.1. Questions about survivor benefits, burial, or similar matters.
   A18.11.2. Compensation-related questions dealing with insurance, gratuities, unpaid pay and allow-
   ances. The CAR providing assistance will address these subjects.
   A18.11.3. Questions relating to mortuary affairs. The mortuary affairs representative will address
   these issues.
   A18.11.4. Questions relating to line of duty, negligence, errors in judgment or the responsibility of
   other personnel concerned with the incident.
   A18.11.5. Your prior experiences or personal conjectures.
   A18.11.6. In short, limit your discussion to the information contained in the notification letter and do
   not discuss matters that you are not qualified to discuss.

A18.12. After the Notification.
   A18.12.1. Confirm the NOK’s address is correct and obtain their telephone number for future con-
   tact.
   A18.12.2. Ask the NOK if they wish to personally notify other immediate family members or have
   them notified by the Air Force.
238                                                       AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


         A18.12.2.1. If the NOK wants to notify other family members, encourage them to do so before
         you depart the residence.
             A18.12.2.1.1. Advise the NOK to contact HQ AFPC/DPFCS at their toll-free number
             (1-800-433-0048), as soon as possible after notifications to other family members have been
             completed.
         A18.12.2.2. If the NOK prefers the Air Force notify other family members, telephone HQ AFPC/
         DPFCS at their toll-free number (1-800-433-0048), as soon as possible from the NOK’s area, but
         not from their home, and provide the names, addresses, and telephone numbers of those family
         members.
      A18.12.3. Stay with the NOK as long as needed, but depart the residence in a professional manner
      and within a reasonable period of time.
         A18.12.3.1. If at all possible, do not leave the NOK alone.
         A18.12.3.2. Encourage the NOK to contact a relative, neighbor or friend to stay with them, or ask
         if they want you to do it for them.

A18.13. Verifying the Notification.
      A18.13.1. Immediately after departing the NOK’s location, but before returning to your base, home,
      or unit, telephone HQ AFPC/DPFCS at 1-800-433-0048, to report the following information:
         A18.13.1.1. Time notification was completed.
         A18.13.1.2. NOK’s name, address and telephone number.
         A18.13.1.3. Any unusual events or comments by the NOK.
         A18.13.1.4. Name(s), relationship to the member, address(es), and telephone number(s) of other
         family members to be notified by the NOK or the Air Force.
      A18.13.2. Return to the MPF and provide the above information to the CAR.

A18.14. Additional Contacts Between You and the NOK.
      A18.14.1. Under normal circumstances, you will not have any further contact with the NOK. An
      exception might occur when a military member is initially declared DUSTWUN. In this case, you
      may be initially called upon to notify the NOK of this status and again later, if the member is declared
      deceased or missing. NOTE: Your personal actions will directly affect the outcome of the casualty
      notification and will set the stage for future assistance to the NOK.
AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007                                                                     239

and they will put you in touch with your (husband’s; wife’s; son’s; daughter’s; father’s; or mother’s) com-

                                            Attachment 21

     PREPARING AF IMT 58, CASUALTY ASSISTANCE SUMMARY (TRANSMITTAL)

A21.1. Purpose.
   A21.1.1. The official historical record of all actions during the casualty reporting, notification and
   assistance process.
   A21.1.2. Used to keep an account of casualty assistance provided to the NOK of deceased and miss-
   ing Air Force members, to include active duty, ANG, USAFR, and retiree deaths.
   A21.1.3. Used to answer inquiries received from NOK, members of Congress, or senior leadership
   concerning notification procedures, assistance, or receipt of benefits years after the case is closed.
   A21.1.4. Used to transfer and/or administratively close a casualty case file.

A21.2. General.
   A21.2.1. The CAR must ensure that:
       A21.2.1.1. The AF Form 58 is typed and entries are completed accurately.
       A21.2.1.2. An extensive explanation is provided when a benefit is denied or disapproved.
       A21.2.1.3. The dates benefits applied for and received are recorded in items 10A through 10J.
   A21.2.2. If space does not permit a sufficient explanation in items 1 through 10W, cross-reference the
   entry to item 12 and explain fully.
   A21.2.3. Item 12 is used to explain items difficult to resolve.
   A21.2.4. Ensure item 11 includes each contact made with individuals to whom assistance is provided.
       A21.2.4.1. The form must be completed in a manner that is easily read and understood.
   A21.2.5. When NOK move and the case is transferred, it is the responsibility of the gaining base to
   ensure the losing base provides sufficient information to accurately continue completing the form.
   A21.2.6. The instructions in this attachment are not all-inclusive. The CAR must use good judgment
   in determining the appropriate remarks.
   A21.2.7. Use bond paper for continuation sheets, if needed. Place the member's name, grade, and
   SSN at the top of the paper.

A21.3. Item-by-Item Instructions for Active Air Force, ANG, and USAFR Casualties (Missing or
Deceased) and Retirees
   A21.3.1. Item 1—Name (Last, First, Middle Initial). Self-explanatory.
   A21.3.2. Item 2—SSN. Self-explanatory.
   A21.3.3. Item 3—Grade. Self-explanatory.
NOTE: Items 1 through 3 must agree with the information on the final DD Form 1300.
   A21.3.4. Item 4—Date of Death. Self- explanatory. Does not apply to missing persons.
242                                                       AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


      A21.3.5. Item 5—Date First Contact Made To NOK. Self-explanatory. Indicate the date initial con-
      tact was made with the NOK.
      A21.3.6. Item 6:
         A21.3.6.1. Active. If the casualty died on active duty, place an “X” in the block.
         A21.3.6.2. Retired, Date of Retirement. If the casualty died after retirement, place an “X” in the
         block and type in the date of retirement.
      A21.3.7. Item 7—Manner/Cause of Death. Must agree with the confirmed manner and cause of death
      on the final DD Form 1300 or civilian death certificate. Does not apply to missing persons. EXAM-
      PLE: Illness: Heart Attack.
      A21.3.8. Item 8A—Name, Relationship, and SSN. Be sure to show the person's relationship and
      SSN.
      A21.3.9. Item 8B—Address (Include ZIP Code) and Phone. Enter the address and phone number of
      the NOK only when you close the case.
      A21.3.10. Item 8C—Minor Children (Name, SSN, DOB, Address and Guardian if other than widow/
      er):
         A21.3.10.1. List those children who were unmarried and under 18 years of age at the time the Air
         Force declared the member deceased or missing.
         A21.3.10.2. Ensure SSN, date of birth, and address for each child is shown.
         A21.3.10.3. If the child does not reside with the widow/er, include the name of the guardian.
         A21.3.10.4. If child(ren) listed on the DD Form 1300 is/are not listed in this item because of mar-
         ital status or age, make a note of it in item 12.
      A21.3.11. Item 9—Parents - Date Assistance Letter Forwarded (if parents are not listed in Item 8):
         A21.3.11.1. Enter the date the benefit advice letter is sent to the parents.
         A21.3.11.2. Does not apply to missing persons.
      A21.3.12. Item 9A—Name and Address of Father. Self-explanatory. If deceased, enter “Deceased.”
      A21.3.13. Item 9B—Name and Address of Mother. Self-explanatory. If deceased, enter “Deceased.”
      A21.3.14. Item 9C—Name, Relationship and Address of Others Assisted (Continue in Item 12).
      Self-explanatory.
      A21.3.15. Items 10A through 10V—Enter Dates/Appropriate Comment (When assisting more than
      one person, indicate name and respective dates each benefit was applied for and received):
         A21.3.15.1. Does not apply to missing persons.
         A21.3.15.2. Follow these instructions carefully:
             A21.3.15.2.1. State the reason whenever you use the term "Ineligible."
             A21.3.15.2.2. If assisting more than one person, include the name of the person applying for
             and receiving each benefit.
             A21.3.15.2.3. Use item 12 to continue your remarks.
AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007                                                                243


  A21.3.16. Item 10A—Death Gratuity:
     A21.3.16.1. For members who die on AD, ADT, or IDT:
        A21.3.16.1.1. Payment is delivered by the CAR within 24 hours of the member’s death,
        unless the NOK desires other arrangements.
        A21.3.16.1.2. Payment for minor children is made by DFAS-CL within 30 days after they
        receive the required claim form along with supporting documentation.
        A21.3.16.1.3. For additional information see paragraph 4.9. and Table 4.2.
        A21.3.16.1.4. In the “Applied” block, enter the date you applied to the local FSO or mailed
        the claim form, and supporting documentation to DFAS-CL for payment.
        A21.3.16.1.5. In the “Received” block, enter the date NOK received payment.
     A21.3.16.2. For retirees who die within 120 days after retirement:
        A21.3.16.2.1. Payment is made by DFAS-CL only after the VA determines death was caused
        by an illness or injury incurred while the retiree was on AD, ADT, or IDT.
        A21.3.16.2.2. For additional information see paragraphs 4.29., 4.34., and Table 4.3.
        A21.3.16.2.3. If the beneficiaries are eligible:
            A21.3.16.2.3.1. In the “Applied” block, enter the date claim form and supporting docu-
            mentation, were mailed to DFAS-CL.
            A21.3.16.2.3.2. In the “Received” block, enter the date NOK received payment, or state
            why they are not eligible. EXAMPLE: “Ineligible - Death not service-related.”
            A21.3.16.2.3.3. If retired over 120 days enter “Ineligible – Retired over 120 days”
  A21.3.17. Item 10B—Unpaid Pay and Allowances:
     A21.3.17.1. In the “Applied” block, enter the date the claim form and supporting documentation,
     were mailed to DFAS for processing.
     A21.3.17.2. In the “Received” block, enter the date payment was made to the beneficiary.
     A21.3.17.3. If the member was ineligible, state the reason. EXAMPLE: "Ineligible--Indebted to
     USAF."
     A21.3.17.4. For additional information, see paragraphs 4.11., 4.31. and 4.51., and Table 4.2. and
     Table 4.3..
  A21.3.18. Item 10C—SBP and RSFPP:
     A21.3.18.1. In the “Applied” block, enter the date the claim forms and supporting documentation
     were mailed or faxed to Defense Finance and Accounting Service - Cleveland Center (DFAS-CL)
     or DFAS, U. S. Military Annuitant Pay, P. O. Box 7131, London, KY 40742-7131 for processing,
     or for active duty members with no eligible dependents, “No Eligible Dependents.” For retirees,
     enter “Declined Coverage.” as appropriate.
     A21.3.18.2. In the “Received” block, enter the date the spouse or eligible children started receiv-
     ing the annuity payment or the date DFAS established the annuity. Never annotate “DIC Exceeds”
244                                                       AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


         or “N/A” as a claim must be filed and established in every case when there is an entitlement
         regardless of the amount of the annuity.
         A21.3.18.3. For additional information see paragraphs 4.13., 4.32., 4.52. and 4.53. and Table 4.2.
         and Table 4.3.
         A21.3.18.4. RCSBP for ANG and USAFR:
         A21.3.18.5. If the deceased completed the satisfactory years of service to qualify for retired pay
         at age 60 and made an election within 90 days of notification of eligibility to participate in the pro-
         gram, in the “Applied” block, enter the date the claim forms and supporting documentation were
         mailed to Defense Finance and Accounting Service, U. S. Military Annuitant Pay, P. O. Box 7131,
         London KY 40742-7131 for processing or “N/A” as appropriate.
         A21.3.18.6. In the “Received” block, enter the date the spouse or eligible children started receiv-
         ing the annuity payment.
         A21.3.18.7. If the deceased did not complete the satisfactory years of service, or make an election
         within 90 days of notification of eligibility to participate in the program, in the “Applied” block
         enter “Ineligible—Years of Service” or “No election made.”
         A21.3.18.8. For additional information see paragraphs 4.14., 4.33. and 4.54., and Table 4.2. and
         Table 4.3..
         A21.3.18.9. In all cases when the benefit is not applicable to the member type “N/A.”
      A21.3.19. Item 10D—DIC and VA Pension:
         A21.3.19.1. DIC:
            A21.3.19.1.1. In the “Applied” block, enter the date the claim form and supporting documen-
            tation were mailed to the VARO.
            A21.3.19.1.2. In the “Received” block, enter the date the NOK received either their first
            check or an award letter.
            A21.3.19.1.3. If the VA denies the claim, enter “Denied—Death not service-related.”
            A21.3.19.1.4. If the NOK does not want to apply, enter “Counseled—(date)/Not desired.”
            A21.3.19.1.5. When assisting parents, if the VA denies the claim based on their income, enter
            “Denied—Income exceeds VA limit.” (VA determines eligibility based on the parents’
            income.)
            A21.3.19.1.6. If assisting parents, do not use:
                A21.3.19.1.6.1. “Ineligible—Relationship.” (Their relationship makes them eligible).
                A21.3.19.1.6.2. “Ineligible—Not dependent.” (Parents do not have to be dependent on the
                member to be eligible.)
            A21.3.19.1.7. For additional information see paragraphs 4.16., 4.34. and 4.57., and Table 4.2.
            and Table 4.3..
AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007                                                                 245


     A21.3.19.2. VA Pension (Non-service-Connected Death Pension):
        A21.3.19.2.1. In the “Applied” block, enter the date the claim form and supporting documen-
        tation, were mailed to the VARO.
        A21.3.19.2.2. If the VA denies a pension, state the reason. EXAMPLE: "Denied—Income
        exceeds VA limit."
        A21.3.19.2.3. If the beneficiaries receive DIC, they are ineligible for the VA pension, enter
        "Ineligible—DIC Awarded."
        A21.3.19.2.4. For additional information see paragraphs 4.17., 4.35. and 4.58., and Table 4.2.
        and Table 4.3..
  A21.3.20. Item 10E—SGLI, VGLI, and NSLI/SDVI:
     A21.3.20.1. SGLI:
        A21.3.20.1.1. If the deceased member had coverage in effect:
            A21.3.20.1.1.1. In the “Applied” block, enter the date the claim form and supporting doc-
            umentation were mailed to HQ AFPC/DPFCS.
            A21.3.20.1.1.2. In the “Received” block, enter the date the beneficiary received the pay-
            ment.
     A21.3.20.2. If the deceased member had no coverage in effect, enter “See item 12,” and indicate
     the reason in item 12.
     A21.3.20.3. VGLI:
        A21.3.20.3.1. Enter “None.”
     A21.3.20.4. SDVI:
        A21.3.20.4.1. If the deceased member did not have coverage, enter “None.”
        A21.3.20.4.2. If the deceased member had coverage in effect:
            A21.3.20.4.2.1. In the “Applied” block, enter the date the claim form and supporting doc-
            umentation were mailed to the VARO and Insurance Center for processing.
            A21.3.20.4.2.2. In the “Received” block, enter the date beneficiary received payment.
        A21.3.20.4.3. For additional information, see paragraphs 4.18., 4.36., 4.37., 4.59., 4.60., and
        4.61., and Table 4.2. and Table 4.3..
  A21.3.21. Item 10F—SS Lump Sum and SS Monthly:
     A21.3.21.1. SS Lump Sum:
        A21.3.21.1.1. If assisting the surviving spouse, or if no surviving spouse, the oldest child eli-
        gible for or entitled to Social Security benefits during the month of the member’s death:
            A21.3.21.1.1.1. In the “Applied” block, enter the date the NOK visited the Social Security
            office and applied for the lump sum death payment.
            A21.3.21.1.1.2. In the “Received” block, enter the date the NOK received payment.
246                                                    AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


         A21.3.21.2. For additional information, see paragraphs 4.20., 4.40. and 4.65., and Table 4.2. and
         Table 4.3..
         A21.3.21.3. If the person being assisted isn’t eligible for the SS Lump Sum payment, type “Ineli-
         gible – Not Dependent.”
         A21.3.21.4. SS Monthly:
            A21.3.21.4.1. If the person being assisted is ineligible for Social Security monthly payments,
            indicate the reason. EXAMPLES: "Ineligible--spouse under age 60" or "Ineligible—Insuffi-
            cient coverage."
            A21.3.21.4.2. If assisting the member's spouse and children and the spouse is ineligible but
            the children are eligible, show the applied for and received dates.
            A21.3.21.4.3. If assisting the member’s parents, they must be at least age 62 and have been
            dependent on the member for more than 50 percent of their support. If the parents are ineligi-
            ble, state the reason. example: "Ineligible—Not dependent."
                A21.3.21.4.3.1. Do not use "Ineligible—Relationship." Their relationship does not make
                them ineligible.
            A21.3.21.4.4. If the NOK being assisted is eligible for Social Security monthly payments:
                A21.3.21.4.4.1. In the “Applied” block, enter the date the NOK visited the Social Security
                office and applied for the monthly payments.
                A21.3.21.4.4.2. In the “Received” block, enter the date the NOK started receiving the
                monthly payments.
         A21.3.21.5. For additional information, see paragraphs 4.19., 4.39. and 4.64., and Table 4.2. and
         Table 4.3..
      A21.3.22. Item 10G—180 Days BAH:
         A21.3.22.1. For active duty members only:
            A21.3.22.1.1. Eligible family members occupying government housing on the date of death
            may continue to occupy housing without charge for 180 days.
                A21.3.22.1.1.1. If they vacate before the 180 days are up, the BAH is paid for the remain-
                ing unused days.
            A21.3.22.1.2. Eligible family members not occupying government housing on the date of
            death, may receive BAH or an overseas housing allowance for 180 days.
            A21.3.22.1.3. In the “Applied” block, enter the date unpaid pay and allowances were applied
            for.
            A21.3.22.1.4. In the “Received” block, enter the date the NOK received payment.
                A21.3.22.1.4.1. If the person applying for the unpaid pay and allowances is ineligible for
                BAH, enter “Ineligible—Not dependent”
            A21.3.22.1.5. For additional information, see paragraph 4.12.
AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007                                                                247


     A21.3.22.2. For retirees:
         A21.3.22.2.1. Enter "Ineligible—Retired."
  A21.3.23. Item 10H—ID Card:
     A21.3.23.1. In the “Applied” block, enter the date eligible NOK applied for their new ID cards.
     A21.3.23.2. In the “Received” block, enter the date eligible NOK received their new ID cards.
     A21.3.23.3. If you are assisting someone who was not an eligible family member of the deceased,
     enter “Ineligible—Not dependent.”
     A21.3.23.4. See paragraphs 4.21.4.4., 4.41.4.4. and 4.66.4.4.
  A21.3.24. Item 10I—VA Education:
     A21.3.24.1. If the deceased member contributed to this program, the VA will pay a special Mont-
     gomery GI Bill death benefit to the designated beneficiary of the member’s SGLI if death was ser-
     vice connected (Line of Duty - Yes).
     A21.3.24.2. The deceased must either have been entitled to educational assistance under the
     Montgomery GI Bill Program or a participant in the program who would have been so entitled but
     for the high-school diploma or length-of-service requirement.
     A21.3.24.3. The death benefit is paid to the member’s designated beneficiary for SGLI.
     A21.3.24.4. Submit a letter along with the SGLV 8286 (SGLI Election and Certificate) and a
     copy of the DD Form 1300, Report of Casualty, to the VARO in paragraph 4.15., 4.38. and 4.63.
     A21.3.24.5. In the “Applied” block, enter the date the letter and supporting documentation were
     mailed to the appropriate VARO.
     A21.3.24.6. In the “Received” block, enter the date the benefit was received.
     A21.3.24.7. If the NOK is not eligible to apply for and receive the death benefit refund, enter "N/
     A."
     A21.3.24.8. For additional information, see paragraphs 4.15., 4.38. and 4.63. and Table 4.2. and
     Table 4.3..
  A21.3.25. Item 10J—Thrift Savings Plan (TSP).
     A21.3.25.1. Determine if the member was contributing to the TSP through the local FSO.
     A21.3.25.2. Apply for the proceeds to the beneficiary on TSP-17 form. Mail the application to the
     address indicated on the form.
     A21.3.25.3. Enter the date the application was completed and forwarded and the date it was
     received by the beneficiary.
     A21.3.25.4. If the beneficiary is someone other than the primary NOK, enter the name and rela-
     tionship in the “Additional Comments” section.
  A21.3.26. Item 10K-Posthumous Decoration:
     A21.3.26.1. Enter the date of presentation or “None presented” as appropriate.
  A21.3.27. Item 10L-Lapel or Gold Lapel Button (Pin).
248                                                     AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


         A21.3.27.1. Enter date presented to NOK.
         A21.3.27.2. If more than one button/pin was presented, list recipients in Section 12, “Additional
         Comments.”
      A21.3.28. Item 10M—Dependent Travel through Item 10W—Legal Assistance:
         A21.3.28.1. Counsel the NOK on each benefit and possible entitlement in accordance with Chap-
         ter 4 of this AFI and AFPAM 36-3028.
         A21.3.28.2. Enter the date counseled or “N/A,” if ineligible.
NOTE: Counsel the NOK on all relevant interment benefits, including Department of Veterans Affairs
burial benefits, and headstone allowances.
      A21.3.29. Item 11—Chronological Listing of Contacts:
         A21.3.29.1. Enter all contacts with NOK, applicable agencies, and any other contacts pertinent to
         the case.
         A21.3.29.2. Contact the NOK of a deceased retiree:
            A21.3.29.2.1. By telephone or in person within 24 hours of learning of the casualty.
            A21.3.29.2.2. At least once every 30 days for the first 2 months.
            A21.3.29.2.3. At least once every 60 days starting with the 3rd month until the NOK receives
            all benefits or the case is closed.
            A21.3.29.2.4. At other times, based on problems encountered and the NOK’s desires.
      A21.3.30. Item 12—Additional Comments:
         A21.3.30.1. Enter continuation remarks from any item listed on the front side of this form, includ-
         ing the item number.
         A21.3.30.2. Use this block to record the reason for any denied benefit.
      A21.3.31. Items 13 and 14:
         A21.3.31.1. Self-explanatory.
         A21.3.31.2. The CAR closing the case will sign the form.

                                              Attachment 22

                       SAMPLE BENEFIT ADVICE LETTER TO PARENTS
(Appropriate Letterhead)
Unit Mailing Address                                                                                (date)
Mr. and Mrs. Jack Smith
1234 Main Street
Austin, Texas 78002
Dear Mr. and Mrs. Smith
       I was very sorry to learn of the death of your son, Lieutenant Colonel Joe P. Smith.
        My office helps the next of kin of Air Force members apply for government benefits they may be
entitled to as the result of a member's death. We have been helping your daughter-in-law, Mrs. Jane M.
Smith, apply for her benefits and privileges.
        In certain circumstances, parents are also eligible for benefits from the Social Security Adminis-
tration and the Department of Veterans Affairs (VA). Based on your son’s earnings, for you to be eligible
for Social Security benefits you must be at least 62 years of age and you must have been dependent on him
for over one-half of your support at the time of his death. If you believe you may be eligible, you should
contact the nearest Social Security office. Your son's social security account number is 123-45-6789.
        Regardless of dependency, if your combined annual income is less than ______ (excluding any
income you are receiving from the VA), you may be eligible for VA Dependency and Indemnity Com-
pensation. This depends on the VA determining that Colonel Smith's death was service related. The VA is
currently deciding this issue on behalf of his widow. If you believe you may be eligible, you should con-
tact the nearest VA office.
        If you have any questions, or if I may be of assistance to you, please do not hesitate to call my
office at (210) 123-4567.
                                                      Sincerely


                                                      FREDERICK P. SCHWARTZ
                                                      Casualty Assistance Representative

SAMPLE LETTER TO THE NEXT OF KIN OF A DECEASED RETIREE WHEN ASSISTANCE
                       IS ACCOMPLISHED BY MAIL
(Appropriate Letterhead)
Unit Mailing Address                                                                                   (date)
Mrs. Jane M. Smith
1235 Main Street
Austin, Texas 78002
Dear Mrs. Smith
         Please accept my deepest condolences on the death of your husband, Master Sergeant Joe P.
Smith.
        My office helps the next of kin of Air Force members apply for government benefits they may be
entitled to as a result of a member's death. Sergeant Smith's Air Force retired pay stopped as of the date of
his death; however, there are _____ days pay due for the month in which he died. For your convenience,
I have attached SF 1174, Claim for Unpaid Compensation of Deceased Member of the Uniformed
Services. Please complete this form, have your signature witnessed by two people, and return the form to
me with a copy of Sergeant Smith's death certificate, I will see that the Defense Finance and Accounting
Service-Denver Center receives your claim. We will keep you advised of the status of your claim.
        Prior to his death, Sergeant Smith elected an annuity for you under the Survivor Benefit Plan.
Effective the day after his death, you are eligible to receive 55 percent of the base amount that he elected
for you, if you are under age 62. If you are age 62 or older, your annuity will be either 35 percent of the
base amount your spouse elected or offset by the amount of Social Security entitlement earned while your
spouse was on active duty, whichever is greater. Please complete the attached DD Form 1884, Applica-
tion for Annuity Under the Retired Serviceman's Family Protection Plan (RSFPP) and/or Survivor
Benefit Plan (SBP), and return this form to me.
        One of the items you will need is a new DD Form 1173, Uniformed Services Identification and
Privilege Card. To obtain the card, you will need to visit the Military Personnel Flight, Customer Service
Element, in building 100. Their office hours are 7:30 a.m. to 4:30 p.m., Monday through Friday. You will
need to bring a copy of the death certificate, your marriage certificate, and Sergeant Smith’s retirement
order. If you have minor children, please include copies of their birth certificates. If there are other eligi-
ble dependents, please call this office and we will advise you of the documents required to issue them new
DD Forms 1173.
        Also enclosed for your information is Air Force Pamphlet 36-3028, Benefits and Entitlements for
Family Members of Retired Air Force Deceased, and VAP 80-XX-1, Federal Benefits for Veterans and
Dependents. These pamphlets contain basic information and criteria, and list agencies available to assist
you in submitting various benefit claims. I strongly recommend that you also contact the Social Security
Administration and the Department of Veterans Affairs (VA) for information on other possible benefits.
       If you have questions or need help completing the attached forms, do not hesitate to call me. My
telephone number is (210) 123-4567 and my office hours are from 8 a.m. to 5 p.m., Monday through Fri-
day.

Dear Mr. and Mrs. Jones
       Please accept my deepest condolences at the tragic death of your daughter,

        At the time of the accident, Lori was performing her duties as flight engineer on a C-130 aircraft.
The aircraft was scheduled to fly a navigational training mission, taking off from Hill Air Force Base,
Utah, with a scheduled landing at the same base 4 hours later. Shortly after takeoff, the aircraft departed
its controlled flight pattern and crashed in the Wasatch mountains, east of the base.
        Your daughter was a fine Air Force crewmember who was well liked by everyone here in the
wing. Her love of flying led to the establishment of many friendships and associations. We all feel a per-
sonal loss in her untimely death.

                                             Attachment 26

                SAMPLE CIRCUMSTANCE LETTER - DUSTWUN TO MISSING
(Appropriate Letterhead)
Unit Mailing Address                                                                               (date)
Mrs. Susan A. Hanes
2436 Sunrise Boulevard
San Antonio, Texas 78232
Dear Mrs. Hanes
        It is with deep regret that I write to inform you that the status of your husband has been changed
from whereabouts unknown to missing. As I have explained, whereabouts unknown is a transitory duty
status which provides a commander with additional time to decide on the most accurate status for a mem-
ber. Since no additional information surfaced during our extensive search for John's aircraft, and I remain
unsure of his true status, I have declared him missing.
        The Air Force continued the search efforts I previously described to you until yesterday, when we
concluded that no evidence remained that search aircraft or naval vessels could detect within the range of
John’s aircraft. We searched an area of approximately 80,000 square miles, with concentrated efforts in
the area that would most likely have contained wreckage. Both the US Air Force and the US Navy dedi-
cated many aircraft to the search. Some commercial airlines and numerous Civil Air Patrol aircraft also
participated in the search. Electronic surveillance of the search area will continue for the next 2 weeks.
Please be assured that if I receive any new information concerning your husband's status, I will notify you
immediately.
        I am compiling a detailed report containing all known information concerning the incident. This
report should be complete within 5 days, at which time I will forward it to the Air Force Missing Persons
Branch. That office will provide you with additional information and will keep you informed of all future
developments concerning John's status.
       If you wish to correspond with the Missing Persons Branch, you may write to AFPC/DPFCM, 550
C Street West, Suite 15, Randolph AFB TX 78150-4717, or call 1-800-531-5501.
        On behalf of John's many friends in the 345th Tactical Fighter Wing, please accept my deepest
condolences during this time of anxiety. If I can be of personal assistance, please contact me at any time
at (210) 652-XXXX.
                                                     Sincerely
                                                     JAMES J. HUGHES
                                                     Brigadier General, USAF
                                                     Commander

        Please accept my deepest condolences at the tragic death of your son, First Lieutenant Henry A.
Jones, Jr., on 9 May 1998. His loss saddened the members of this organization. I want to explain the cir-
cumstances that led to Henry’s death as we understand them.
        Henry had walked to the bus stop with Stacey and Nicole to see them off to school. After they
were on their way, Henry began jogging and had run for about two blocks when he collapsed. He went
into convulsions and was given cardiopulmonary resuscitation by a passing motorist while an ambulance
was being summoned. Henry was transported to the Good Samaritan Hospital in Tampa, Florida, where
he was pronounced dead on arrival from an apparent heart attack.
       You should be very proud of your son. He was a fine young man who was certainly well liked by
everyone. Henry's achievements were many. His dedication to duty led to the establishment of many
friendships and associations. We all feel a great personal loss in his untimely death.

                                              Attachment 29

                     SAMPLE CIRCUMSTANCE LETTER - COMBAT DEATH
(Appropriate Letterhead)
Unit Mailing Address                                                                                 (date)
Mrs. John A. Smith
111 Pine Street
San Antonio, Texas 78232
Dear Mrs. Smith
        Please accept my heartfelt condolences on the death of your husband, Major John A. Smith. John
was highly respected by the members of the 111th Fighter Wing, both for his exceptional leadership abil-
ities and his skill as a pilot. I want to explain the circumstances surrounding John’s death as we under-
stand them at this time.
         John departed Riyadh Air Base at 9:00 a.m. on the morning of March 30 to conduct a visual recon-
naissance mission in a heavily defended, hostile area. After completing a series of reconnaissance runs
and accomplishing an in-flight refueling, he returned to the target area to continue his mission. During the
flight, the aircraft encountered enemy gunfire, and the navigator reported that he heard two loud explo-
sions. Despite the navigator’s continued attempts to contact him, no contact was made. The navigator
flew the aircraft to a safe area and elected to eject both himself and John rather than to attempt a landing.
The ejection was successful; however, John had already suffered fatal injuries. It was determined that he
died instantly as a result of enemy ground fire.
       His gallantry on this mission was typical of the outstanding devotion he has demonstrated
throughout the past 8 months. I am proud to have been associated with John, and I join with the rest of the
wing in expressing our deepest condolences at his loss. Be assured that I stand ready to help you in any
way I can during this time of sorrow.
                                                      Sincerely


                                                      WILLIAM A. BROWN
                                                      Brigadier General, USAF
                                                      Commander

try is founded grow stronger each day by the dedication to duty from military professionals such as Ser-
geant Smith.


                                                    Sincerely


                                                    WILLIAM A. BROWN
                                                    Brigadier General, USAF
                                                    Commander

A34.1. If the primary assistance CAR is located in the CONUS, Hawaii, or Alaska and is responsi-

         Address the documentation to the VSO by name, if known, and stamp the package with "DO NOT
         OPEN IN THE MAIL ROOM."
         A34.1.1.2. HQ AFPC/DPFCS, 550 C Street West, Suite 14, Randolph AFB TX 78150-4716.

                                              Attachment 35

                            FORMAT FOR ANG/USAFR DEATH REPORT

A35.1. General.
      A35.1.1. This report is designated emergency status C-2.
      A35.1.2. Continue reporting during emergency conditions, normal precedence.
      A35.1.3. Continue reporting during MINIMIZE.

A35.2. Format.
      A35.2.1. Report on those persons listed in Table 6.1.
      A35.2.2. Enter the addressees and locations indicated in Table 6.1.

A35.3. Specific Instructions.
      A35.3.1. Prepare the message in easily readable tabular form, with each item lettered and beginning
      on a new line at the left margin.
      A35.3.2. All reports must contain items A, B, and C.
      A35.3.3. Label unknown or unconfirmed items as "UNKNOWN" or "UNCONFIRMED" and con-
      firm them as soon as possible in a supplemental report.
      A35.3.4. Never report a person's death as unconfirmed.
      A35.3.5. Reference the initial Death Report on all supplemental reports.

A35.4. Message Precedence.
      A35.4.1. Use ROUTINE for all addressees on initial and supplemental reports (see Table 6.1.).

A35.5. Subject Line of Message Report. Enter CASUALTY REPORT: INITIAL DEATH REPORT
(HAF-SV(AR)9471) or SUPPLEMENTAL DEATH REPORT (HAF-SV(AR)9472) (Duty Status).

A35.6. Item-by-Item Instructions.
      A35.6.1. Item A—Name of Casualty.
         A35.6.1.1. Enter the last name.
         A35.6.1.2. Repeat the last name.
         A35.6.1.3. Enter the first name, middle name, and suffix, if any.
         A35.6.1.4. EXAMPLE: JOHNSON, REPEAT JOHNSON, CLAYTON EMERSON, JR.
      A35.6.2. Item B—Grade.
         A35.6.2.1. Enter the member's military grade.
         A35.6.2.2. If the Air Reserve Component plans to posthumously promote the member, state
         "YES" and include the special order number, date, and issuing headquarters.
AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007                                                             265


        A35.6.2.2.1. EXAMPLE: STAFF SERGEANT, YES, SPECIAL ORDER G-12, 12 MARCH
        1998, HQ ARPC.
  A35.6.3. Item C—Social Security Number (SSN).
     A35.6.3.1. Enter the member's SSN and repeat.
     A35.6.3.2. EXAMPLE: 123-45-6789, REPEAT 123-45-6789.
  A35.6.4. Item D—Organization, MAJCOM, and Installation.
     A35.6.4.1. Enter the complete name of the member's unit and installation of assignment, includ-
     ing Army, Air Force, or Fleet Post Office (APO or FPO).
        A35.6.4.1.1. Do not abbreviate.
        A35.6.4.1.2. For non-participating members or retired Reserve members, state "HQ ARPC."
        A35.6.4.1.3. EXAMPLE: 9 11 TA G, A F R E S , G R E AT E R P I T T S B U R G H I A P PA
        15231-5000.
        A35.6.4.1.4. State whether ANG member is AGR, Traditional or Technician.
            A35.6.4.1.4.1. EXAMPLE: 156 FG, MUNIZ ANG BASE, CAROLINA, PR, TRADI-
            TIONAL.
  A35.6.5. Item E—Place of Death.
     A35.6.5.1. Enter the specific place of death (city and state or country).
     A35.6.5.2. Enter the name and title of the person who officially pronounced the member dead.
     A35.6.5.3. EXAMPLES:
        A35.6.5.3.1. PRONOUNCED DEAD ON ARRIVAL AT ST. JOHN’S HOSPITAL, CLEVE-
        LAND OH, BY DR LUIS GARCIA.
        A35.6.5.3.2. PRONOUNCED DEAD AT THE SCENE, 2 MILES SOUTH OF ROTH TX
        ON FORM 278, BY MEDICAL EXAMINER, DR JOHN SMITH.
  A35.6.6. Item F—Date and Time of Death.
     A35.6.6.1. Enter the local date and approximate time.
     A35.6.6.2. If the member was discovered dead and the date of death is questionable, indicate
     "FOUND" and the date and time the member was found.
     A35.6.6.3. If the member and the member's spouse both die in the same incident, report the con-
     firmed time of death for each.
  A35.6.7. Item G—Cause of Death.
     A35.6.7.1. If there is no confirmed manner and cause of death, report the preliminary determina-
     tion and label it "UNCONFIRMED."
     A35.6.7.2. Confirm the cause of death in a supplemental report when known. Include the source
     of confirmation, such as a death certificate or autopsy report.
     A35.6.7.3. For a natural death, report both the primary and underlying cause, using medical
     terms.
266                                                     AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


         A35.6.7.4. For a death report on a member whose remains were not recovered, give the apparent
         cause. EXAMPLE: "APPARENT DROWNING—REMAINS NOT RECOVERED."
      A35.6.8. Item H—Date, Time, and Source of Notification to Unit.
         A35.6.8.1. Enter the local date, time, and who notified the unit of the member's death.
         A35.6.8.2. For ANG members, furnish brief account of circumstances leading to death.
      A35.6.9. Item I—Name and Address of NOK.
         A35.6.9.1. Enter the name and address of the member's NOK.
         A35.6.9.2. For ANG members, list family members wanting an ANG Memorial Certificate.
      A35.6.10. Item J—Persons Notified or To Be Notified.
         A35.6.10.1. State if the NOK has been notified of the member's death.
         A35.6.10.2. If the NOK has not been notified of the member’s death, state whether you need
         AFPC/DPFCS to make a personal notification.
             A35.6.10.2.1. EXAMPLE: "REQUEST AFPC/DPFCS MAKE NOTIFICATION TO THE
             FOLLOWING PERSONS: (Indicate name, relationship, address and any other pertinent infor-
             mation)."
      A35.6.11. Item K—Casualty Assistance.
         A35.6.11.1. Enter "THE REPORTING UNIT IS (OR IS NOT) PROVIDING CASUALTY
         ASSISTANCE TO (name and relationship)."
         A35.6.11.2. If the reporting unit is not providing casualty assistance, request that HQ ARPC
         assume assistance responsibility.
      A35.6.12. Item L—Reporting Unit.
         A35.6.12.1. Enter the complete name of your organization; do not abbreviate.
         A35.6.12.2. Enter your name, grade, and DSN or commercial telephone number including area
         code.
         A35.6.12.3. For ANG members, supplement message from Attachment 2, paragraphs A2.6.12.
         through A2.6.20., (items M through U) as needed.

                                             Attachment 38

                PREPARING DD FORM 93, RECORD OF EMERGENCY DATA

A38.1. General.
   A38.1.1. Entries explained below are for electronic or typewriter completion, except those specifi-
   cally noted.
      A38.1.1.1. If a computer or typewriter is not available, print in black or blue-black ink ensuring a
      legible image on all copies.
          A38.1.1.1.1. Complete a new form when a computer or typewriter becomes available.
   A38.1.2. The preprinted instructions on the reverse side of the paper copies do not apply to the Air
   Force.
   A38.1.3. When the space for a particular item is insufficient, insert “See #13” and continue the infor-
   mation in item 13.
      A38.1.3.1. See A38.2.27. for preparation instructions for item 13.
   A38.1.4. Do not use correction fluid, paper correction tape, or typewriter lift-off correction tape on
   any originals; complete a new form.
   A38.1.5. The DD Form 93 is used as an interim form only until the member completes a vRED.
   Instructions for completing the vRED are contained within the program on the web site.

A38.2. Item-by-Item Instructions.
   A38.2.1. Item 1—Member’s Name:
      A38.2.1.1. Enter, using uppercase letters, the member’s last name, first name, and middle
      name(s).
      A38.2.1.2. If there is no middle name, enter "NMN."
      A38.2.1.3. If there is only a middle initial, enter "IO" (initial only).
      A38.2.1.4. Include "JR.," "SR.," "III" or similar designation.
      A38.2.1.5. Do not extend the name into the SSN block - Continue in Block 13..
   A38.2.2. Item 2a—Member’s Social Security Number (SSN). Enter the member’s SSN.
   A38.2.3. Item 2b—Initial. Leave this item blank.
   A38.2.4. Item 3a—Service. Leave this item blank.
   A38.2.5. Item 3b—Reporting Unit Code/Duty Station. Leave this item blank.
   A38.2.6. Item 4a—Spouse’s Name:
      A38.2.6.1. Enter, using uppercase letters, the spouse's first name and middle initial (see para-
      graphs A38.3.1., A38.3.2., A38.3.3. and A38.3.5.).
      A38.2.6.2. Enter, using uppercase letters, the spouse’s last name only if it’s different from the
      member's last name.
270                                                      AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


         A38.2.6.3. If the member is not married, enter his/her specific marital status.
            A38.2.6.3.1. EXAMPLES: “ SINGLE,” "DIVORCED," or "WIDOWED."
      A38.2.7. Item 4b—Spouse’s Address:
         A38.2.7.1. Enter the spouse’s physical (not mailing) address and include the appropriate ZIP code
         (see paragraphs A38.3.4. and A38.3.5.).
      A38.2.8. Item 5a—Children’s Name:
         A38.2.8.1. Enter, using uppercase letters, the children’s first names and middle initials, to include
         adult children, and illegitimate children if acknowledged by member or paternity/maternity has
         been judicially decreed (see paragraphs A38.3.1., A38.3.2., A38.3.4., and A38.3.5.). NOTE: The
         DD Form 93 is used for making timely notifications to all family members and designated benefi-
         ciaries listed, to include adult and illegitimate children.
         A38.2.8.2. Enter the child’s last name only if it is different from the member’s.
         A38.2.8.3. If none, so state.
      A38.2.9. Item 5b—Children’s Relationship to Service Member.
         A38.2.9.1. Enter the relationship to the servicemember using either clear-text, abbreviations or
         the following codes:
            A38.2.9.1.1. “03” for son (S).
            A38.2.9.1.2. “04” for daughter (D).
            A38.2.9.1.3. “13” for stepson (SS).
            A38.2.9.1.4. “14” for stepdaughter (SD).
            A38.2.9.1.5. “33” for adopted daughter (AD).
            A38.2.9.1.6. “34” for adopted son (AS).
            A38.2.9.1.7. “88” for other, such as ward (W).
      A38.2.10. Item 5c—Children’s Date of Birth:
         A38.2.10.1. Enter the date of birth by YYYY/MM/DD. EXAMPLE: 19800915.
      A38.2.11. Item 5d—Children’s Address.
         A38.2.11.1. Enter each child's address following these guidelines (see paragraphs A38.3.4. and
         A38.3.5.):
            A38.2.11.1.1. If the address is the same as the current spouse, enter "SAME AS ITEM 4b."
            A38.2.11.1.2. If a minor child does not reside in the same household as the member, enter the
            full address, including the name of the person the child lives with and that person’s relation-
            ship to the member. If no such relationship exists, state the relationship between the child and
            the person the child lives with (e.g., CHILD’S MOTHER.).
            A38.2.11.1.3. If a child is an adult, state that the child resides independently and provide the
            full address.
AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007                                                              271


        A38.2.11.1.4. If the member is a single parent and children reside in the same household as
        the member, state that children reside with the member and provide the full address.
        A38.2.11.1.5. EXAMPLES:
            A38.2.11.1.5.1. “KIMBERLY J/14/19800915/SAME AS ITEM 4."
            A38.2.11.1.5.2. "ERIC C/03/19820103/ RESIDES WITH MEMBER’S FORMER
            SPOUSE SALLY S. SMITH AT 123 MAIN ST, OKAY, OK 12345."
            A38.2.11.1.5.3. "JOHN J/03/19830419/RESIDES WITH CHILD'S NATURAL
            MOTHER, SUSAN B. JONES AT 567 TEMPLE AVE, SWISS COLONY, AR 12456."
            A38.2.11.1.5.4. "SUSAN N/04/19870817/RESIDES WITH MEMBER AT 4435 SHER-
            WOOD WAY, SAN ANTONIO TX 78212."
            A38.2.11.1.5.5. “MARY A. JOHNSON/04/19700807/RESIDES INDEPENDENTLY
            AT 7734 OAK FORREST LANE, DALLAS TX 76521.”
  A38.2.12. Item 6a—Father’s Name:
     A38.2.12.1. Enter, using uppercase letters, the first name, middle initial, last name of the mem-
     ber’s natural father (see paragraphs A38.3.1., A38.3.2., A38.3.3., and A38.3.5.).
     A38.2.12.2. If the member’s natural father is deceased, enter "DECEASED," followed by stepfa-
     ther's first name, middle initial, last name, if applicable.
     A38.2.12.3. If the member does not know their natural father’s name, enter “MEMBER DENIES
     ALL KNOWLEDGE OF NATURAL FATHER.”
  A38.2.13. Item 6b—Father’s Address:
     A38.2.13.1. Enter the natural father’s address and include the appropriate ZIP code (see para-
     graphs A38.3.4. and A38.3.5.).
     A38.2.13.2. If the member does not know his or her natural father’s address, enter “WHERE-
     ABOUTS UNKNOWN,” followed by his or her stepfather’s address, if applicable (see paragraphs
     A38.3.4. and A38.3.5.).
     A38.2.13.3. If the member knows his or her natural father’s name but not the address, enter the
     appropriate statement, followed by his or her stepfather’s address if applicable (see paragraphs
     A38.3.4. and A38.3.5.).
  A38.2.14. Item 7a—Mother’s Name:
     A38.2.14.1. Enter, using uppercase letters, the first name, middle initial, last name of the mem-
     ber’s natural mother (see paragraphs A38.3.1., A38.3.2., A38.3.3., and A38.3.5.).
     A38.2.14.2. If the member’s natural mother is deceased, enter "DECEASED," followed by step-
     mother's first name, middle initial, last name, if applicable.
     A38.2.14.3. If the member does not know their natural mother’s name, enter “MEMBER
     DENIES KNOWLEDGE OF NATURAL MOTHER.”
272                                                       AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


      A38.2.15. Item 7b—Mother’s Address:
         A38.2.15.1. Enter the natural mother’s address and include the appropriate ZIP code (see para-
         graphs A38.3.4. and A38.3.5.).
         A38.2.15.2. If the member does not know his or her natural mother’s address, enter “WHERE-
         ABOUTS UNKNOWN,” followed by his or her stepmother’s address, if applicable (see para-
         graphs A38.3.4. and A38.3.5.).
         A38.2.15.3. If the member knows his or her natural mother’s name but not the address, enter the
         appropriate statement, followed by his or her stepmother’s address if applicable (see paragraphs
         A38.3.4. and A38.3.5.).
      A38.2.16. Item 8a—Do Not Notify Due to Ill Health:
         A38.2.16.1. List relationship to the servicemember of person(s) listed in items 4a, 5a, 6a or 7a
         who are not to be notified of a casualty due to ill health.” EXAMPLE: "MOTHER."
         A38.2.16.2. If the Record of Emergency data lists more than one child, specify which child the
         Air Force should not notify. EXAMPLE: "DAUGHTER, SUSAN."
         A38.2.16.3. If not applicable, enter "NONE."
      A38.2.17. Item 8b—Notify Instead:
         A38.2.17.1. If the person is already listed on the form, enter relationship to the service member.
         EXAMPLE: “FATHER.”
         A38.2.17.2. If the person is not listed on the form, enter the name, relationship to the servicemem-
         ber, and address of person(s) to be notified in lieu of person(s) listed in item 8a (see paragraphs
         A38.3.1.
         A38.2.17.3. Do not indicate an individual living at the same residence as the person listed in item
         8a.
         A38.2.17.4. If brothers or sisters are designated, show date of birth (YYYYMMDD). EXAM-
         PLE: 19800915.
      A38.2.18. Item 9a—Beneficiary(ies) for Death Gratuity:
         A38.2.18.1. Enter the first name, middle initial, last name, and relationship to the servicemember
         of person(s) to receive the death gratuity pay if there is no surviving spouse or child at the time of
         death (see paragraphs A38.3.1. through A38.3.3.).
         A38.2.18.2. Only parents (including stepparents or a person acting in loco parentis), brothers and
         sisters (including those of half-blood and those through adoption) may be designated.
             A38.2.18.2.1. In loco parentis means any person(s) who acted in place of the member’s par-
             ent(s) for a period of not less than 1 year at any time before the member entered on active duty.
             A38.2.18.2.2. If brothers or sisters are designated, show date of birth (YYYYMMDD).
             EXAMPLE: 19800915.
         A38.2.18.3. Enter "NONE" if the member has no eligible beneficiary, or does not wish to desig-
         nate a beneficiary, in which case payment is made in the order of precedence established by law.
AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007                                                               273


     NOTE: Title 10, U.S.C. Annotated, Armed Forces, Chapter 75, Death Benefits, Section 1477,
     does not provide for the designation of an "alternate" beneficiary for the death gratuity.
     A38.2.18.4. The member should make specific designation as it expedites payment.
         A38.2.18.4.1. If the member makes no designation, prior to death of the member, the case
         must be referred to DFAS-DE for settlement.
  A38.2.19. Item 9b—Address for Beneficiary(ies) for Death Gratuity:
     A38.2.19.1. Enter the address for each person listed and include the appropriate ZIP code (see
     paragraphs A38.3.4. and A38.3.5.).
  A38.2.20. Item 9c—Percentage To Be Paid Beneficiary(ies) for Death Gratuity:
     A38.2.20.1. If only one person is designated, enter "100%."
     A38.2.20.2. Show percentage to be paid to each person if two or more beneficiaries are desig-
     nated. The sum of the shares must equal 100 percent. EXAMPLE: 50% EACH.
         A38.2.20.2.1. If no percentage is indicated and more than one person is named, the money is
         paid in equal shares to the persons named.
  A38.2.21. Item 10a—Beneficiary(ies) for Unpaid Pay and Allowances:
     A38.2.21.1. The member may designate anyone to receive this payment.
     A38.2.21.2. Enter the first name, middle initial, last name, relationship to the servicemember, of
     person(s) to receive the member’s unpaid pay and allowances (see paragraphs A38.3.1. through
     A38.3.3.).
     A38.2.21.3. If the member does not wish to designate a beneficiary, enter “NONE.”
     A38.2.21.4. The member is urged to designate a beneficiary for unpaid pay and allowances as
     payment will be made to the person in the order of precedence established by law (Title 10, U.S.C.
     Annotated, Armed Forces, Chapter 165, Accountability and Responsibility, Section 2771).
     A38.2.21.5. If brothers or sisters are designated, show date of birth (YYYYMMDD). EXAM-
     PLE: 19800915.
  A38.2.22. Item 10b—Address for Beneficiary(ies) for Unpaid Pay and Allowances:
     A38.2.22.1. Enter the address for each person listed and include the appropriate ZIP code (see
     paragraphs A38.3.4. and A38.3.5.).
  A38.2.23. Item 10c—Percentage To Be Paid Beneficiary(ies) for Unpaid Pay and Allowances:
     A38.2.23.1. If only one person is designated, enter "100%."
     A38.2.23.2. If the member designated two or more beneficiaries, state the percentage to be paid
     for each. The sum of the shares must equal 100 percent. EXAMPLE: 50% EACH.
     A38.2.23.3. The beneficiary for unpaid pay and allowances can be anyone the member elects to
     receive the proceeds. However, monies cannot be paid directly to a minor. If the beneficiary is a
     minor whose birth date and guardian is not included elsewhere on the form, include the benefi-
     ciary's date of birth (YYYYMMDD). EXAMPLE: 19900915, and the name of the minor's adult
     guardian.
274                                                        AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007


      A38.2.24. Item 11—Allotment Designee/Percentage If Missing. Leave this item blank. Since the Air
      Force does not use Item 11, the member does not sign INSTRUCTION TO SERVICE MEMBER on
      the top portions of the form.
      A38.2.25. Item 12a—SGLI. Leave this item blank.
      A38.2.26. Item 12b—Insurance Companies/Policy Numbers (Optional). Enter full name of all life
      insurance companies and the policy numbers (see paragraph A38.3.5.).
      A38.2.27. Item 13—Continuation/Remarks:
         A38.2.27.1. Use this space for continuation of other items or remarks, if necessary. Prefix entry
         with the number of the item being continued. EXAMPLE: 5/JOHN J./03/19830419/567 TEMPLE
         AVE, SWISS COLONY, AR 12456.
         A38.2.27.2. Use this item to list name, address, and relationship of other persons the member
         desires to be notified (see paragraphs A38.3.1. through A38.3.4.).
         A38.2.27.3. Other family members may also be listed in this item.
      A38.2.28. Item 14—Signature of Servicemember:
         A38.2.28.1. Have the member check and verify all entries on the form and sign in blue or black
         ink.
         A38.2.28.2. The member should sign first name, middle initial, last name, and grade.
      A38.2.29. Item 15—Signature of Witness:
         A38.2.29.1. Have a disinterested witness sign in blue or black ink.
         A38.2.29.2. The witness should sign first name, middle initial, last name, and grade.
      A38.2.30. Item 16—Date Signed. Have the member date in blue or black ink using this format:
      YYYYMMDD EXAMPLE: 19980701.

A38.3. NOTES:
      A38.3.1. If the individual listed speaks or understands little or no English, enter his/her principal lan-
      guage.
         A38.3.1.1. EXAMPLE: "PRINCIPAL LANGUAGE: SPANISH." Do not repeat if already stated
         in a preceding item.
      A38.3.2. If the person listed in the item is a military member, include grade, branch of service, unit
      and base of assignment.
         A38.3.2.1. EXAMPLE: SMSGT/USAF/RANDOLPH AFB TX.
      A38.3.3. If retired military, enter "RETIRED GRADE AT TIME OF RETIREMENT, AND
      BRANCH OF SERVICE.
         A38.3.3.1. EXAMPLE: "RETIRED/LT COL/USA." Do not repeat if already stated in a preced-
         ing item.
AFI36-3002_50SWSUP_I 10 OCTOBER 2007                                                                275


  A38.3.4. Never show the address as “UNKNOWN:”
     A38.3.4.1. If the member cannot provide a current address, enter the last known address and
     the approximate year it was valid. Review the member’s UPRG for documents containing
     addresses of NOK.
     A38.3.4.2. Advise the member that if they know a person having knowledge of the current
     address, they must obtain it and complete a new DD Form 93 within 30 days. The preparer must
     establish a 30-day suspense to ensure the member completes the form with current or last known
     address.
     A38.3.4.3. If the member absolutely cannot obtain the address, as a last resort only, enter
     “MEMBER UNAWARE OF WHEREABOUTS AT ANY TIME". Advise the member of the Air
     Force’s responsibility to make personal notification to the people listed on the form.
     A38.3.4.4. Addresses shown as P.O. Box Numbers or RT or RFD numbers should indicate in
     Item 13, “Continuations/Remarks” a street address or general directions to reach the place of resi-
     dence.
     A38.3.4.5. If the member cannot provide directions, enter “DIRECTIONS UNKNOWN.”
     A38.3.4.6. If the address for the person in the item has been shown in a preceding item, it is
     unnecessary to repeat the address, enter “SAME AS ITEM (and the preceding item number) ___.”
     EXAMPLE: SAME AS ITEM 4b.
  A38.3.5. When the space for a particular item is insufficient, enter “SEE #13” and continue the infor-
  mation in item 13.
